Salesforce Technology & Products  
**Secret Decoder Ring** (glossary / index) ATO  
Short URL for this page: [http://sfdc.co/**decoder**](http://sfdc.co/decoder) 		See Also: [https://sfdc.co/sfdc-acronyms](https://sfdc.co/sfdc-acronyms)   [https://sfdc.co/glossaryhubhome](https://sfdc.co/glossaryhubhome)

| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| **Term** | **Definition** | **For More Info** |
| 1a, 1b, 2a, 2b, 3a, 3b, 4a, etc | Date range convention used in Sprint names. Digits are month number (1=Jan, etc), a is first half of month, b is second half of month. **Note:** some teams use two-week sprints instead of half-month sprints, so a third sprint in a given month is possible, with a c instead of an a or b. |  |
| 202, 204, 206, 208, m210, 212, 214... | Name of a build, upgrade release of Salesforce app stack. Three per year. | [Release Calendar](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1AJIesgtJlyiWmpcH1xS036r3gP2_ZbK62ZwDGXLJy2Y/edit#gid=0) Builds in GUS:  [204](https://gus.my.salesforce.com/a06B0000000Bu8N)  [206](https://gus.my.salesforce.com/a06B0000000Bu8O)  [208](https://gus.my.salesforce.com/a06B0000000Bu8P)  [210](https://gus.my.salesforce.com/a06B0000000Bu8Q) See also “WRoR” below |
| 2PC | Two-Phase Commit \[Protocol\] | ([wikipedia](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Two-phase_commit_protocol)) |
| 2RR | **Deprecated \-** now “TMP Roadmap Summit” (Apr 2019\) Two-Release Roadmap \-- a planning doc showing what a team is doing in the next two upcoming releases. | ([TMP Roadmap Summit](https://gus.lightning.force.com/lightning/r/CollaborationGroup/0F9B000000000v7KAA/view)) ([chatter group \- infrastructure, FY19](https://gus.lightning.force.com/lightning/r/CollaborationGroup/0F9B00000009LXZKA2/view)) |
| 222 (2:2:2, 2-2-2) | Infra Data Science initiative to reduce lead time of new insights from 2 months down to 2 hours within 2 years. | ([Chatter post](https://gus.my.salesforce.com/0D5B000000RgyAB)) |
| 333 (3:3:3, 3-3-3) | Compute Cloud initiative to reduce host allocation time from three seasons to three minutes within three years. | ([3:3:3 Chatter Home](https://gus.my.salesforce.com/_ui/core/chatter/groups/GroupProfilePage?g=0F9B00000006QZ6)) |
| 3AZ | A design shift away from having complete “primary and DR” instances to instead have the primary spanned across three Availability Zones within a region. | ([AWS Availability Zones](https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AWSEC2/latest/UserGuide/using-regions-availability-zones.html)) |
| 3ER | “... a robust java application known as 3-Eyed Raven. It is a service in which we use to backup/restore internal SDB, Oracle database and host filesystem in SFDC.” (From [the SA.](https://gus.lightning.force.com/lightning/r/ADM_Security_Assessment__c/a7YB000000002aUMAQ/view) | [SFDC Backup & Restore Architecture](https://docs.google.com/presentation/d/1CJs87pvb1Z6GDTs6J3XGMdxLDvTyd4qyUm9oENQoWNg/edit#slide=id.g35104f7bc1_2_295) |
| 3PAO | Third-Party Assessment Organization |  |
| 3PP | Third-Party Products \- a team and process to review any SFDC-external code or software you want to use... | ([Chatter homepage](https://gus.my.salesforce.com/_ui/core/chatter/groups/GroupProfilePage?g=0F9B0000000006s)) |
| 4H | History, Heroes, Heartbreaks and Highlights \-- categories for a person to describe who they are, e.g. to teammates.See also Life Map below. | \[[Deck](https://docs.google.com/presentation/d/1SM4cC2O-JK5YfKcjHfqSSKKNjXpcFyYNRLLpSTPBUlU/edit#slide=id.g797474f6b0_1_2131)\] |

| ACDC | Automated Control for Data Centers | [http://sfdc.co/acdc](http://sfdc.co/acdc) ([ACDC Chatter home](https://gus.my.salesforce.com/_ui/core/chatter/groups/GroupProfilePage?g=0F9B000000008Af)) |

| ACS | API Cursor Service (aka "TemStore") \- multi-tenant data store for opaque data (“blobs”) temporarily persisted (not just cached) with typical TTL between 30 minutes and 2 weeks. Replaced by Vagabond. | See Vagabond below |

| AILTN | App log record type for Lightning user activity events |  |
| AIR | Availability Insights Reporting \-- standardized health reporting including READS | \[[Chatter](https://gus.lightning.force.com/lightning/r/CollaborationGroup/0F9B00000009r0SKAQ/view)\]  \[[Confluence](https://confluence.internal.salesforce.com/pages/viewpage.action?pageId=217134843)\] |
| AirFetch | Falcon service that brings log data files from Jump Cloud back to the Salesforce Commercial environment | \[[Quip](https://salesforce.quip.com/adSaADbSDIHd#temp:C:XHZ6005a0283f5b4b26b1b8882cf)\] |
| AirFilter | A service that determines which build artifacts should vs should not be propagated across an Air Gap into a “high side” sensitive environment | \[[Quip](https://salesforce.quip.com/vDzaAa5HceZn)\] |
| Airflow | (aka Apache Airflow) open source “...platform to programmatically author, schedule and monitor workflows” | [https://airflow.apache.org](https://airflow.apache.org) |
| Air Gap, Airgap | An instance of some software that runs without any network connectivity to/from that instance \-- an air gap instead of network (no wireless, no ethernet, no fiber) \- for security, to reduce attack surface area. See “blackjack” | [https://sfdc.co/blackjack](https://sfdc.co/blackjack) |
| Airlock | Services, process and tooling for moving artifacts (code binaries, config files etc) from “low side” where they are built up to “high side” \- isolated production runtime. | \[[Confluence](https://confluence.internal.salesforce.com/pages/viewpage.action?spaceKey=AIRGAP&title=The+Airlock)\] |
| AirSuite | Tooling (AirFilter, AirTrust) for governance, trust and validation in support of processes and standards that meet cross-zone transfer requirements \- for Blackjack and Alibaba. | \[[Quip](https://salesforce.quip.com/adSaADbSDIHd)\] |
| AirTrust | A Falcon service that receives bundle requests from AirFilter and handles chain of trust concerns. | \[[Quip](https://salesforce.quip.com/0udaA9DvPc40#OdGAAAH7SMv)\] |
| Ajna | Cloud/suite of services offering Kafka for Salesforce, and Mirus/Ajna Direct for data pipelining. Often known for providing key components included by the MonCloud metrics/logs/events/traces pipelines.   | ([Ajna Ingestion chatter home](https://gus.my.salesforce.com/_ui/core/chatter/groups/GroupProfilePage?g=0F9B000000043aw)) |
| Ajna Kafka | Kafka services for Salesforce, including multi tenancy and tenant management, for pubsub and pipelining and supporting internal and external use cases and features. |  |
| Ajna Mirus | SFDC-internal service to replicate Ajna Kafka data to local blob storage (ex S3, GCS), with additional aggregation (ex regional) offerings.  | ([announced](https://gus.lightning.force.com/one/one.app#/sObject/0D5B000000d1ihKKAQ/view)) |
| AKC | Argus Kubernetes Cluster \- the EKS cluster within Falcon Monitoring FD’s that hosts Argus | Contact: Kirankumar Gowdru |
| AKS | Azure Kubernetes Service | ([Azure AKS](https://azure.microsoft.com/en-us/services/kubernetes-service/)) ([Comparison w/AWS, Google](https://gus.lightning.force.com/one/one.app#/sObject/0D5B000000l5B9mKAE/view)) |
| Alation | Company and software product for data science.Also, specific SFDC-internal instance of this provided by PDS and IT. | ([Concierge \- alation onboarding](https://concierge.it.salesforce.com/articles/en_US/Supportforce_Article/Alation-Onboarding)) [https://alation.com/](https://alation.com/)  |
| Alcatraz | Project focusing on Security Detection at scale | ([Chatter home](https://gus.my.salesforce.com/0F9B0000000CvXF)) |

| Allowlist | (fka whitelist) list of entities a service will process, as opposed to a blocklist (see below) | \[[Post](https://gus.lightning.force.com/lightning/r/0D5B000000yqoZMKAY/view)\] ([wikipedia](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Whitelist)) |

| MTTD | Mean Time To Detect: average duration from the time any failure begins until a person (on-call) becomes aware of that problem, for all incidents in some period of time. | [Confluence: Definition of TTx Metrics](https://confluence.internal.salesforce.com/display/SR/Definition+of+TTx+Metrics) |
| MTTE | Mean Time To Engage: average duration from the time a customer acts to contact the on-call person until success, for all incidents in some period of time. | [Confluence: Definition of TTx Metrics](https://confluence.internal.salesforce.com/display/SR/Definition+of+TTx+Metrics) |
| MTTM | Mean Time To Mitigate: average duration for a providing team to reduce impact to customers to an acceptable level. | [Confluence: Definition of TTx Metrics](https://confluence.internal.salesforce.com/display/SR/Definition+of+TTx+Metrics) |
| MTTR | Mean Time To Resolve: average duration for an issue to be resolved for all incidents in some period of time. | [Confluence: Definition of TTx Metrics](https://confluence.internal.salesforce.com/display/SR/Definition+of+TTx+Metrics) |
| MVP | Minimum Viable Product \- smallest feature set needed to go live in a limited way, to learn pivotal facts about customers. | ([wikipedia](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Minimum_viable_product)) |

| S3 | Amazon’s Simple Storage Service, block store. Also an API similar to other store services (See Lego above) | [https://aws.amazon.com/s3/](https://aws.amazon.com/s3/) ([difference between S3, S3A, S3N](https://stackoverflow.com/questions/33356041/technically-what-is-the-difference-between-s3n-s3a-and-s3)) |
| S3A | File system build over S3, successor to the S3 Native (s3n fs) \- uses Amazon's libraries to interact with S3. Supports files \>5GB, higher performance. All objects accessible from s3n:// URLs should also be accessible from s3a simply by replacing the URL schema. |  |
| S3N | Native filesystem for reading and writing regular files on S3. Advantage of this filesystem is that you can access files on S3 that were written with other tools. Conversely, other tools can access files written using Hadoop. Disadvantage: 5GB limit on file size imposed by S3. |  |
| S3Guard | S3Guard is an experimental feature for the S3A client of the S3 object store, which can use a (consistent) database as the store of metadata about objects in an S3 bucket. | ([Hadoop documentation @ Apache](https://hadoop.apache.org/docs/r3.1.1/hadoop-aws/tools/hadoop-aws/s3guard.html)) |
